## Phase 3 — i18n Structure Review

- Current library: `i18next` + `react-i18next` (from `src/i18n/setup.js`)
- Uses single `translation` namespace object per language: **unknown**
- Merges platform translation packs: **no**
- Merges app-local translation packs: **no**
- Observed structure is workable but not fully scalable yet because many UI strings are still hardcoded in components instead of key-based lookups.
- Key naming is mixed across imports (platform domains + app domains) and is not yet fully feature-complete for all screens.
- Missing/underrepresented dedicated namespaces for broad areas like `settings`, `profiles`, `dashboard`, `learning`, and some `vport` flows.

## Phase 4 — Key Standardization Proposal

- Convention: lowercase dot notation
- Group by feature first: `menu.*`, `reviews.*`, `settings.*`, `profiles.*`, `feed.*`, `booking.*`, `vport.*`
- Avoid sentence keys; use concise semantic keys
- Keep interpolation placeholders explicit (e.g. `{{count}}`)
- Keep one canonical key per intent, reuse across UI to reduce duplication

Sample target shape:

```json
{
  "menu.addItem": "Add item",
  "menu.deleteItem": "Delete item",
  "reviews.noReviews": "No reviews yet",
  "settings.account.deleteAccount": "Delete account"
}
```

## Phase 5 — Safe Migration Plan

1. Freeze new hardcoded UI strings via lint rule or PR checklist (no new literal UI text unless justified).
2. Migrate feature-by-feature in thin PRs (`settings` → `profiles` → `feed` → `vport` etc).
3. For each feature PR:
- Add keys to `en.json`/`es.json`.
- Replace literals with `t("feature.key")`.
- Keep fallback defaults where needed (`t("key", "English fallback")`) during transition only.
4. Add screenshot regression checks on high-traffic screens after each batch.
5. Remove temporary fallbacks once coverage is complete and validated.

## Phase 6 — Spanish Preparation

- `en.json` generated with normalized keys for extracted user-visible strings.
- `es.json` generated with neutral LATAM Spanish translations (auto-assisted; human review recommended for nuanced product tone).

## Phase 7 — Suggested Refactor Examples

Before:

```jsx
<button>Add item</button>
```

After:

```jsx
<button>{t('menu.add_item')}</button>
```

Before:

```jsx
<p>No reviews yet</p>
```

After:

```jsx
<p>{t('reviews.no_reviews_yet')}</p>
```

## Phase 8 — Optional UX Copy Improvements (Report Only)

- Standardize destructive CTA wording: always use `Delete` vs mixed `Remove`/`Erase`.
- Normalize loading states to one style: `Loading…` or `Please wait…`, not both.
- Consolidate empty states: `No results yet` + actionable next step (`Try changing filters`).
- Use consistent tone for confirmations (short, direct, modern).
